This is done by surrounding it, either vertically, horizontally, or diagonally (or a combination of all three). when the entire board is filled or when no side can make a valid move.\r\n* The winner of the game is the one with the most discs when the game is over.\r\n\r\nNOTES: Ultima Reversi has an \"Auto
